Because of the angle, the big bed is facing the mountain view outside the window. It rained heavily on the first night of stay. In the morning, the electric curtains slowly opened, and I was suddenly amazed. I only saw the clouds and mist in the mountains outside the window, which was as beautiful as a Chinese painting (see Figure 8).
The hotel breakfast variety is not too much, but the taste is good. The hotel package I bought also gave a double dinner, which tasted fresh, salty and slightly spicy, which suited my taste. When I went to order food on the second day, the dishes were quite clean, but there was a bowl of mixed noodles that was a bit dry, and the quality needs to be improved.
The hotel is located next to Lingfeng Mountain, which is convenient to walk or drive. The road to Lingfeng Temple is so beautiful, it is simply a green palace! Lingfeng Temple is very quiet, you can get incense for free, and there is a thousand-year-old ginkgo tree in front of the door. Staying in a modern and comfortable hotel, taking a slow walk in the towering trees, and resting in the ancient temples is a perfect vacation combination...

msg:Design:
The hotel's design team is P49 Deesign from Thailand.
P49 also designed the Indigo in Seminyak, Bali, the Indigo in Lijiang Ancient Town, and the Indigo in Moonlight City, Shangri-La.
The design concept of this hotel in Anji is "one blue, one white, one Zen, and one master".

Room:
Sookie at the front desk was really great. As soon as we arrived at the hotel, she helped us upgrade our room type to "Anji White Tea". The service was also very thoughtful during the period!
The room has curved walls, including the closet against the wall at the entrance, which looks like a rolling tea field.
The head of the bed is also in the shape of a bamboo tube, and even the children's slippers have bamboo patterns, which is very cute.
What I like most about this room type is that the bed is placed at an inclined angle, which makes the room more streamlined.
The bed is completely opposite to the bathroom, and the bathroom door is also very soundproof and lightproof, which does not affect the quality of sleep.

Public area:
Small cinema: There are about a dozen seats, there is a lazy sofa area, and different movies are played every day.
Outdoor swimming pool: Internet celebrity swimming pool, very photogenic.
Indoor children's playground: not big, friendly to young children, with two game consoles, a Lego building area, a TV, and an ocean ball play area. The bathroom is very clean, and the small toilet is also animal-shaped, which is extremely cute.
Outdoor children's playground: There are two floors, with brave roads, slides, swings, and trampolines. Refer to the last picture, it surprised me so much.
Gym: Facing the swimming pool, the view is good.
Dining:
The hotel is not big, so there is only one restaurant. The breakfast is very surprising and can be eaten until 12 o'clock.
Although the variety is not so rich, it is completely sufficient.
I ordered Benedict eggs for two consecutive days, and I also like the toppings on the noodles.
There are also two bars, one is Yunshang Bar, on the balcony on the second floor, specializing in draft beer.
The other is Xiaer Bar, an Internet celebrity cave bar. There are also resident performances every Saturday and Sunday, and the a**osphere is full.

msg:advantage:

1. **The hotel design surprised me: the overall design of the hotel is unique and has a natural style, and the mountain environment and air are also very fresh, giving this place a unique temperament.

2. **I was impressed by the room: The interior decoration of my room was natural and stylish, it had an automatic toilet, and the bathroom was large and spacious, which left a deep impression on me.

3. **Allen, the travel photographer, is professional, good at guiding and mobilizing emotions, he is polite, and he took a lot of photos that can bring us wonderful memories.

shortcoming:

1. **Service needs to be improved: I think the hotel service needs to be improved. The lobby waiter lacks initiative. Although we did not bring a suitcase, we had several handbags. The waiter failed to provide timely luggage assistance, which affected my overall experience. Check-in experience.

2. **Insufficient service in the restaurant: We had dinner at Jiwei twice. There was a shortage of waiters in the restaurant, which caused me to wait for a long time, especially on Saturday night. There were about a dozen tables, but there were only a few waiters. For a long time, no one took the initiative to pour water and ask for orders, so I had to call the waiter multiple times to get service.

3. **Lack of indoor swimming pool: The temperature this week has been below zero, so many activities in the hotel can only be done in the hotel. The hotel's indoor children's playground is very small, with only a mini Lego toy table (there are only a few left in the building block box). A few incomplete building blocks) and a mini ocean ball pool. There is no indoor swimming pool, which makes the experience of staying in the hotel with children in winter lacking a lot of fun. I hope that additions can be considered in the future to provide a more comprehensive service experience.

4. **Toilet soundproofing problem: I found that the soundproofing effect of the toilet in the guest room is poor. I can clearly hear the conversation in the bathroom next door/upper and lower rooms. I can even hear the sound of drunken vomiting in the neighbor's room at night. I am a very light sleeper. This caused some disruption to my rest.

5. **Central air conditioner problem: The central air conditioner cannot adjust the temperature by itself. The room at 24 degrees feels very dry and hot. However, due to the infrared linkage set up in the room, the air conditioner will automatically turn off when the balcony door is opened slightly, making it difficult for me to sleep at night. In order to obtain a comfortable sleeping environment, after I reported it to the front desk, the staff told me that there was no way to adjust it, so the problem I reported could not be solved in time.

6. **Inconsiderate service: The flu has been severe recently, and unfortunately our child got a fever in the middle of the night. In an emergency, I called the front desk for help, but I felt the cold attitude on the other end of the phone. I was disappointed that the front desk only provided a thermometer and lacked the care and enthusiasm that the service should have. In an emergency, hotels are expected to provide more considerate support and care.

7. **Emergency services were not timely: In my anxiety, I could only find a nearby pharmacy online and ask a rider to deliver it. However, when the rider informed me that the medicines had been delivered to the hotel, it took the hotel staff nearly 15 minutes to deliver them to my room. This slow response time is particularly uncomfortable during emergencies and brings extra worry and inconvenience to me and the children. Hopefully the hotel will be more prompt and responsive when dealing with emergencies.

Overall, compared to hotels at this price level, Anji Indigo's hardware is so-so, but its service is really not that good. I personally would not choose to visit again.
